The Unification of Traditional Chinese Medical Practitioners 153

Talks by the Standing Committee of the Citizens Training Council

Since the municipal Traditional Chinese Medicine organizations, such as the Shenzhou Medical Association, the Chinese Medical United Association, and the Traditional Chinese Medicine Society, were ordered by the Citizens Training Council to merge into the Traditional Chinese Medicine Association, a sudden incident occurred the other day in which forty-eight people, including Xu Xiangzuo, declared their withdrawal from the Traditional Chinese Medicine Association. To understand the truth of the matter, a reporter from the Guomin News Agency paid a visit yesterday to Chen Yijun, the Standing Committee member of the Citizens Training Council of the Municipal Party Headquarters, to inquire about his opinion on the matter. He replied as follows (the following is the statement of Committee Member Chen): Upon investigation, the municipal Traditional Chinese Medicine organizations have never had a unified organization. The Shenzhou Medical Association, the Chinese Medical United Association, the Traditional Chinese Medicine Society, and the Traditional Chinese Medicine Association each established their own banner and were not subordinate to each other. In the spring of this year, the Traditional Chinese Medicine Association came to the Party Headquarters to apply for registration. After investigation, it was found that most of the members of the association were also members of the other three associations. The initiators and important personnel of the other three associations had also joined the Traditional Chinese Medicine Association. In order to promote the strength of the Traditional Chinese Medicine organizations, the Party Headquarters approved the association's registration to form a formal legal organization. Subsequently, the remaining associations also came to the Party Headquarters to apply for registration one after another, and were separately instructed to cease activities and merge into the Traditional Chinese Medicine Association for the sake of unification. Currently, the Traditional Chinese Medicine Society has already complied with the Party's order to merge. However, it is rumored that the Chinese Medical United Association has encountered some turmoil due to the accumulated public funds in the association, but it is not yet known for certain. Only the Shenzhou Medical Association has been making excuses, claiming to be an academic organization, different from a professional organization, and has repeatedly come to the Party Headquarters to request registration and exemption from merger. However, after investigation by the Party Headquarters, the Shenzhou Medical Association's actions over the years are inconsistent with the purposes of studying medical principles, etc., as stated in Articles 2 and 3 of its charter. For example, holding regular meetings, studying medical principles, establishing specialized medical schools, publishing medical books and newspapers, establishing hospitals, constructing libraries, compiling medical lectures, holding national medical exhibitions, or displaying and reviewing specialized medical terms to ensure a unified standard, improving the manufacturing methods of pills and powders, publicizing public health, and designing epidemic prevention, etc., have not been carried out one by one. Its important work is only to handle the registration of traditional Chinese medicine practitioners with the Health Bureau twice a year, and its daily work is no more than mediating disputes among colleagues regarding professional matters. Therefore, although it claims to be an academic organization, it is actually a professional organization. Therefore, in order to achieve the unification of Traditional Chinese Medicine organizations and reduce the membership fees of doctors, the Party Headquarters has repeatedly instructed that registration should not be approved and that it should still comply with the merger order. This is the general situation of the case in the past. As for the declaration made by Xu Xiangren the other day to withdraw from the membership of the Traditional Chinese Medicine Association, the reason is actually that during the preparatory meeting of the Traditional Chinese Medicine Association held at the beginning of this month, someone put forward a certain report that seemed to refer to the accumulated public funds of the Chinese Medical Society. In fact, the proposer may have had some misunderstandings. Also, the preparatory meeting of the Traditional Chinese Medicine Association was not reported to the Party Headquarters beforehand, so the Party Headquarters did not send personnel to attend and guide it, which led to the occurrence of the misunderstanding. It was indeed the fault of the association. However, once the misunderstanding between the two parties is explained and clarified, the opinions will be completely eliminated, and the dispute can be resolved immediately, and the merger issue can also be completely completed. Moreover, at a time when the new and old medicine (i.e., traditional Chinese medicine and Western medicine) are fiercely competing with each other, Traditional Chinese Medicine practitioners should unite and work together, deeply study medical theories, and strive to promote and conform to science. On the one hand, it can promote the inherent medical spirit of our country, and on the other hand, it can also adapt to the evolutionary trend of world medical science. This is also an important reason why the Party Headquarters ordered the association to merge and organize.

Minutes of the Meeting of the Wusong Machinery Factory Union 154

Since Wang Chunzu, the general manager, and Li Bowen, the inspector, of the Shanghai-Nanjing-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway General Machinery Factory in Zhanghuabang, Songnan, realized at the end of last year that the contracting system was not only unable to save money for the railway bureau, but also caused the workers to suffer greatly, with only the contractors being able to make a large profit, they specially requested and obtained approval from their superiors to abolish the contracting system and planned to conduct a trial run for half a year. They immediately recruited more than 100 workers and explained that if the results of the trial run were better than the contracting system, they could be promoted to permanent workers after six months. However, eight months have passed now, and no one has been promoted yet. Moreover, during the trial period, the carpentry department alone produced 20 fourth-class cars and 5 steam-powered automobiles. According to accounting, the company can earn a profit of 8,000 yuan, and the results are not bad. Unexpectedly, the railway bureau issued a notice two months ago, intending to restore contracting and recruit people to bid, and the workers did not know the details, which caused misunderstandings and disputes. Later, the workers elected representatives to petition their superiors to abolish contracting, but to no avail. Afterwards, they heard that the bidding was held at the railway bureau on the 23rd of last month, and Wu Cairong won the bid with the lowest price. The workers suspected that Wang, the general manager, and Li, the inspector, intended to restore contracting. On Monday morning at 9 o'clock, during the weekly memorial service at the factory, they proposed to petition their superiors again. At that time, Wang and Li happened to walk to the meeting place, which led to a conflict. The factory director, Ma Erhui, came forward to mediate. Then, the reorganization committee sent two representatives to meet with the Wusong Machinery Factory Union representatives Cai Jinhai and Tang Xinglin, as well as the carpentry representative Wei Derong, to visit Deputy Director Luo of the Shanghai General Affairs Section. After the representatives reported the above situation, Director Luo instructed the representatives to return to Songnan and order the workers to continue working as usual and wait for a solution. Therefore, on Tuesday afternoon after work, the workers went out to the Xujiahui Machinery Factory Union to hold a meeting. 295 craftsmen from various departments attended the meeting. The meeting began at 5 o'clock, with rituals as usual. The temporary chairman was Wang Arong, and the recorder was Zhang Yunhong. After the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting, representative Cai Jinhai reported that Director Luo had stated that Wang, the general manager, and Li Bowen had no authority to abolish or restore the contracting system, and that this was an order from their superiors. The workers had misunderstood and that such misconduct had been discovered. In short, the railway bureau wanted to develop and seek convenience, and now 18 of the most needed vehicles should be built quickly, so they had recruited people to bid in order to expedite the project and ensure that the car bodies were sturdy and well-made, and there was no other intention. Then, Zhu Derong explained to the director that the factory's workers could also build these vehicles quickly and ensure that the project was sturdy and well-made. Director Luo allowed the factory's workers to build the vehicles themselves, but they had to elect two responsible representatives to discuss the procedures with the union representatives before starting work. After the report was completed, the crowd discussed the project matters and elected responsible representatives. By the time the meeting ended, the bell had rung seven times. The dispute can also be said to have come to an end.

Minutes of the Meeting of the Candle Industry Association 155

The Candle Industry Association convened a general meeting at 1 pm on the 3rd to reject the union's request for a salary increase and abolish the old practice of giving away flower candles. 44 members attended, chaired by Tong Guanwen. The agenda was as follows: 1. Discuss the union's letter requesting a salary increase. Resolution: Since the labor-capital conditions of the industry were revised by the Social Bureau in the winter of the 17th year [of the Republic], the capital side has suffered many losses. At this time, when the sales of candles have plummeted, there is no room for negotiation on the union's demands, and a letter should be sent to reject them. 2. The industry has a long-standing practice of giving away flower candles, etc. Although the previous general meeting resolved to cancel it and issued a notice, some colleagues are still hesitant. How should this be resolved? Resolution: Another notice will be published to thoroughly abolish the purpose of giving away. If anyone is found to be acting against the rules, they will be punished according to the public agreement. 3. Discuss other important matters. Resolution: Confidential. The meeting adjourned after the agenda was completed.

Jin Wensi's Mother Passes Away 157

Granted a Month's Leave by the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining

Madam Geng, the mother of Jin Wensi, the Councilor of the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining and the Director of the Shanghai Agricultural Products Inspection Bureau, came from the prestigious Geng family of Yun'jian. She was the younger sister of Geng Daochong, a Secretary in the Qing Ministry of Agriculture. She was not only well-versed in poetry and etiquette but also skilled in calligraphy. For many years, she resided in Beijing with Mr. Jin Qiansun. She had just returned south last year when she suddenly contracted dysentery last month. Despite various treatments, she passed away on the afternoon of October 31 at her old residence at Sandeng Bridge in Pinghu. Director Jin had previously requested leave due to his mother's illness and returned home quickly. Now, due to the pain of losing his mother, he telegraphed the Minister of Agriculture and Mining again and was granted a month's leave.

The Comprador of the Zhibade Wheel Reports on the Xiao Case 163

Hoping the Overseas Chinese Federation Will Provide Detailed Instructions

Willing to Comply Within the Possible Range

The Xiao Clan Support Association Issued a Declaration Yesterday

The case of the Chief and Second Mates of the Dutch Java Company's Zhibade Wheel insulting Ms. Xiao Xinan has aroused public outrage. The Zhibade Wheel recently returned to Shanghai, and the wheel's comprador, He Jinrong, specially invited people from all walks of life to a banquet on the wheel yesterday afternoon to clarify everything. More than a dozen reporters from various newspapers and news agencies attended. The wheel's new owner, Primus, was also present to entertain the guests. First, He Jinrong delivered a speech, detailing the circumstances of Ms. Xiao's experience on the wheel that day. He also said that today's banquet was entirely in his personal capacity to report the truth to everyone. He is also Chinese, and after hearing the news at the time, he deeply hated the rudeness of the Dutch and had no reason to favor them. He also said that the company had dismissed the offending Chief Mate Lan Qi and Second Mate Lei Dima, and the owner, Bailaosi, and the doctor had been demoted to other wheels. The manager of the Xijiang branch officially apologized to Ms. Xiao. As for the legal punishment of the Chief Mate, it should be resolved by the court, and the company has no right to intervene. He heard that the Overseas Chinese Federation and other groups were very dissatisfied with the company's handling of the matter, and it would be best to put forward opinions and provide detailed instructions, and to contact the Shanghai Java Company directly for consultation. Within the possible range of the company, it would be willing to comply with the order. Finally, he led the guests to visit the cabin where Ms. Xiao resided. It is said that Ms. Xiao was introduced to He by her friend on the Haiden Wheel and asked to take care of her along the way. Initially, she lived in Room 33, sharing the room with a Fujianese woman in her forties. After passing Hong Kong, Ms. Xiao moved to Room 35 next door due to seasickness, and lived alone, which led to this unfortunate incident. They dispersed at about 4 pm.

Regarding the incident of Ms. Xiao Xinan of Yixing being insulted abroad, her relatives in Shanghai, Xiao Li, Xiao Kai, Xiao Xu, Xiao Huitian, Xiao Zhaokang, and others, believe that although this matter has received enthusiastic assistance from various maritime groups, it has not yet achieved the goal of punishing the perpetrators. It is by no means enough to merely dismiss the Chief and Second Mates. On the 2nd of this month, a Xiao Clan Support Association was formed. The declaration issued by the association yesterday is recorded as follows: To the Shanghai newspapers, Minister Wang of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Central Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, and party headquarters, legal organizations, and schools at all levels: In recent years, the repeated oppression of our overseas Chinese by Dutch imperialism has been a bitter pill to swallow, and it has not been a matter of one day. Such as the imposition of entry tax on overseas Chinese, the expulsion of overseas Chinese teachers, the prohibition of reading the Three People's Principles, and the refusal to hold memorial weeks, all kinds of bizarre tricks have emerged endlessly, and their ambitions have not been curbed. Now, there has been the occurrence of the insult of Ms. Xiao Xinan. Since the exposure in the newspapers, all compatriots have been outraged. The members of our association, with family ties and a sense of unity, feel particularly indignant at this tragic situation. Ms. Xiao lost her father at a young age and came from a poor family. She studied hard from elementary school to normal school. She is cheerful and courteous to others. She possesses the virtues of diligence, prudence, solemnity, frugality, honesty, and steadiness. She has served in the Central District Experimental School and other schools in the capital, and her teaching achievements are remarkable. Teachers and students deeply admire her. This time, introduced by the Beijing Municipal Education Bureau, she did not hesitate to travel far and wide to serve overseas Chinese education in Southeast Asia. Unexpectedly, she encountered an unexpected disaster on her journey. She was not only rudely insulted by the Dutch but also falsely accused by the doctor, which was extremely dark. Ms. Xiao is over thirty years old and still a virgin. She has aspirations for all directions, but Heaven did not bless her, and she suffered a tragic misfortune. Alas, who does not have sisters, wives, and daughters, who does not have relatives? There are quite a few Chinese women who go to the Dutch colonies, so there may be many who have been insulted in the past but dared not speak out. How can it be enough to merely dismiss the Chief and Second Mates? If it is not thoroughly investigated, not only will the victim's grievances be difficult to redress, but also all Chinese women going abroad will be wary. It is a matter of international prestige and national humiliation. We hope that kind people at home and abroad will uphold justice, express sympathy, and unanimously support and punish the perpetrators. We are eagerly awaiting orders and are at your service.

Record of the Qingyun Lane House Demolition Case Trial 164

Firefighters Witnessed the Event

To Testify in the Next Hearing

At 3:30 PM on the day before yesterday (Tuesday), the Criminal Court No. 2 of the Special District Court held a trial for the house demolition case in Qingyun Lane, North Sichuan Road. Judge Cheng Shangfeng presided. The plaintiff's representatives were lawyers Xue Jiaqi and Wang Zuxun, and the defendant's representatives were lawyers Ding Rong and Chen Zhongyin. In addition to the plaintiff and defendant, the witness Gu Wensheng (Gu, a member of the Second District Party Branch, testified on behalf of Xing Dingcheng, compradore of New Sassoon & Co.) was summoned. The judge ordered the police to first take Xing Dingcheng out and used the method of separate questioning. First, the witness Gu Wensheng was asked about his age and occupation. (Answer) Thirty-six years old, business of Zhenji Real Estate Company. (Question) What position do you hold? (Answer) Manager. (Question) What is your relationship with Xing Dingcheng? (Answer) We are friends, and have known each other for one or two years. (Question) Does Xing Dingcheng come to your place? (Answer) He comes often. (Question) When did he come to your place? (Answer) September 10th, at 9:30. (Question) Do you remember clearly, is it definitely 9:30? Because your position as a witness is very important, you must tell the truth. (Answer) I left home at 9:15 by car to the company, and it was indeed 9:30. (Question) Where is your company, and where do you live? (Answer) The company is on Sichuan Road, and I live on Ma Lang Road in the French Concession. (Question) How long did Xing Dingcheng stay at your place before leaving? (Answer) About an hour. (Question) How many rooms are there in the company, and how many people work there? When Xing Dingcheng came to your place, did anyone else see him? (Answer) The company has two rooms, and five or six people work there. When Xing Dingcheng came, he only talked to me, and did not greet anyone else. (Question) What did Xing Dingcheng come to your place for? (Answer) To discuss land business. There is a piece of land in Qinglian Pavilion on Simalu (Fourth Avenue) that a person named Cheng wants to sell. My company is in the business of buying and selling land, and mortgages, so I wanted to introduce it to Xing Dingcheng. (Question) What clothes was Xing Dingcheng wearing? (Answer) I don't remember clearly. (Question) Did you make an appointment with Xing Dingcheng, or did he come on his own? (Answer) I made an appointment. (Question) When did you make the appointment? (Answer) The day before. (Question) In which room did you and Xing Dingcheng talk? (Answer) In the room inside. (Question) Did you and Xing Dingcheng talk for about an hour? (Answer) About an hour. (Question) Did you know about the Qingyun Lane house demolition on September 10th? (Answer) Yes, I also told Xing Dingcheng about it. (Question) How did you know, and how did you tell Xing Dingcheng? (Answer) I found out after reading the newspaper when I got to the company, so I told Xing Dingcheng and gave him the newspaper to read. At this point, the court ordered the defendant Xing Dingcheng to be brought into court for questioning. (Question) What time was the Qingyun Lane house demolition on September 10th? (Answer) I don't know. (Question) Why don't you know? (Answer) In the business, I only manage receiving rent and mortgages, and nothing else. (Question) Do you manage other businesses? (Answer) I don't manage anything else. (Question) What day did you go to Gu Wensheng's place? (Answer) September 10th, at 9:30 in the morning. (Question) You have a job in the company, can you go out in the morning? (Answer) I don't have much to do in the company, so I can go out at any time. (Question) What did you go to Gu Wensheng's place for? (Answer) To discuss land business. There is a piece of land in Qinglian Pavilion on Simalu owned by a person named Cheng that they want to sell, so I went to Gu Wensheng's place to discuss it. (Question) Did you buy it successfully? (Answer) No, I didn't. (Question) How long did you spend at Gu Wensheng's place? (Answer) Because I looked at the drawings and discussed it, I spent about an hour. (Question) If the land was not bought, what drawings did you look at? (Answer) Just planning and planning. (Question) Was it an appointment to go to Gu Wensheng's place? (Answer) Yes, it was an appointment. (Question) When did you make the appointment? (Answer) I don't remember clearly. (Question) Have you been there before? (Answer) Yes, I often go there. (Question) Do you always go in the morning? (Answer) Sometimes in the morning, sometimes in the afternoon. (Question) Have you been there again after September 10th? (Answer) Yes. (Question) What day did you go again? (Answer) I don't remember if it was the day after or two days later, I just remember that I went again. (Question) Why do you only remember clearly the day of the Qingyun Lane house demolition on September 10th, and why don't you remember the others? (Answer) Because when I returned to New Sassoon & Co. from Gu's place that day, people in the company told me that the houses in Qingyun Lane had been demolished, so I especially remember it clearly. (Question) When did you return to the company? (Answer) Eleven o'clock. (Question) Did you go to Gu Wensheng's place from the company, or from home? (Answer) From home. (Question) What day was the demolition of the house of the plaintiff, Miao She? (Answer) September 10th, at 10:00 AM. (Question) When did the White Russians disperse? (Answer) After being beaten, I went to get a medical examination and report to the police station, so I don't know. (Question) What time did you get back from the medical examination? (Answer) Because I was injured in the head, I was confused and didn't remember clearly when I got back. (Question) When you got back, had you eaten lunch yet? (Answer) I hadn't eaten lunch yet at that time. (Question) What time did the White Russians come to demolish the house on that day, Ye Chenglin? (Answer) A little after ten o'clock. (Question) Had it already struck ten o'clock? (Answer) I didn't pay attention to whether it had already struck. (Question) When did the White Russians disperse? After I was beaten, I went to the police station to report, so I don't know when they dispersed. (Question) Which police station did you go to report to, is it far away? (Answer) To the Hongkou Police Station, not very far. (Question) What time did you get back? (Answer) After eleven o'clock. At this point, Chen Zhongyin, the defendant's representative lawyer, spoke, saying that there was a supplementary statement to be submitted and requested the court to summon the manager of New Sassoon & Co. Judge Cheng replied that the position of the manager of New Sassoon & Co. did not need to be summoned. Lawyer Ding Rong continued, saying that the Fire Brigade had arrived at the scene that day, and two Fire Brigade members knew the situation at the time. I had asked the two firefighters, who said that they had witnessed two Western representatives from New Sassoon & Co. leading the White Russians to demolish the house that morning. One was tall and one was short, and they were Westerners, not Chinese. There was also a Western policeman on the scene who was heard saying to the two Western representatives of New Sassoon & Co. that the house could not be demolished. It was evident that the two firefighters were deeply aware of the situation that day, and requested the court to summon the two firefighters to court to inquire about everything, but the names of the two firefighters did not need to be announced, and I could submit a written record to the court, etc. Judge Cheng asked how he knew the firefighters were so detailed. Lawyer Ding Rong replied that he guessed the firefighters must have been at the scene that day, so he went to investigate and thus knew. At this point, the plaintiff's representative lawyer spoke, saying that on the day of the White Russian house demolition, there must have been disturbances, and the tenants would have blown whistles to report to the police. The Fire Brigade received the report and then sent a car. By the time the fire truck arrived, the White Russians might have already dispersed, so the testimony of the firefighters was unreliable. Lawyer Wang Zuxun continued, saying that on September 10th, whether the White Russian house demolition was a fact, whether Miao Shelai was beaten, whether Ye Chenglin was assaulted and had 20 yuan stolen was a fact, the court should pay attention to it. And whether it is legally permissible for a lawyer to find witnesses for the client. At this point, Judge Cheng announced that the hearing would be adjourned to next Tuesday, and the police station would be ordered to summon the patrolmen on duty that day and the two firefighters. Xing Dingcheng was still released on the original bail, and then the court adjourned.

First Frost Seen This Morning 165

The Weather is Very Cold

Due to the cold air coming in continuously in recent days, the temperature has dropped significantly. As a result, the north has snowfall, and the city is suddenly very cold, as if it were winter. Yesterday's lowest temperature was 7.9 degrees Celsius, more than two degrees lower than the same period last year. Although the high pressure is still sending cold air to this port, it has not stopped. Therefore, there is no hope of warming up during the day. Due to the high pressure of cold air the day before yesterday, the first frost was seen this morning. If the high pressure can move eastward, there will be a hope of warming up during the day. However, because the cold air is coming too fast, the citizens have not had time to prepare cold-weather clothing, so the scene is very difficult.

Bandit's Wife Avenges Her Husband 166

Investigating the Whereabouts of the Bandit Leader

Secretly Reporting to the Police Finally Leads to the Arrest

Qu Chengqing, a clerk at the Tianxiang Foreign Firm at No. 1 Guangdong Road, was kidnapped by bandits at around 11:00 PM on the 11th of this year after drinking with relatives and returning to the back door of his residence at No. 1760 Keneng Road, Haining Road. The bandits intended to extort a large sum of money. Subsequently, on March 18th, the Chinese and foreign detectives of the Huishan Police Station cracked the bandit's den, rescued the hostage Qu Chengqing, and arrested 14 bandits, including Zhang Zhangji and He Qing'en. They were sent to the court for questioning and sentenced. Zhang Zhangji was sentenced to death, He Qing'en to life imprisonment, and the rest were punished separately. However, during the court questioning, Shen A'di, one of the defendants, confessed that Bao Rongtang from Ningbo Tiantai (also known as Lao Er, also a member of the gang) was an accomplice. The court issued an arrest warrant, but it has not been caught for half a year. At around 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, a woman named Zhang Chenshi, claiming to be the wife of the executed Zhang Zhangji, secretly reported to the Chief Inspector's Office of the General Police Station that Bao Rongtang was currently gathering and gambling with friends at No. 4, Lane 386, Gonghe Road, Zhabei. Therefore, Chief Inspector Lu Liankui, detectives Wang Cheng, Wu Changkai, female detective Zhao Shuyun, and Western detective Weilkaosi secretly went to the location, and together with detectives from the Zhabei Public Security Bureau, arrested Bao and brought him back to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Criminal Court No. 2 of the Special District Court. The police station's lawyer Wang Yaotang stated the facts of the case, requested that the case be postponed, and also stated that the informant Zhang Chenshi claimed to live at No. 414, Xinkang Lane, Yangshupu. Zhang Zhangji, who had been executed, was her husband, and the defendant Bao Lao Er was the leader of the kidnapping case. Her husband had been a carpenter, and Bao had invited him three times, claiming to go to "pahei lao" (meaning to rob opium). Her husband believed it was true and went with him. However, Bao changed his tune and kidnapped the plaintiff, hiding him at their place and using a gun to threaten her husband to be a guard. This led to the bandit's den being discovered, and he was sent to your court and sentenced to death, which has not yet been carried out. And Bao is still at large. Although she had searched everywhere, Bao's whereabouts were uncertain, until yesterday when she learned of Bao's location, so she reported to the police to arrest him, etc. When questioned, the defendant Bao Lao Er denied the charges, claiming that Zhang Chenshi was his mistress and that because her husband had committed a crime and been detained, she had repeatedly asked him for money and he had refused, leading to the false accusation. Zhang Chenshi then claimed that the defendant's statement was completely fabricated and that she was purely avenging her husband. If the court did not believe her, they could inquire at the Huishan Police Station about the six or seven people who had been arrested, all of whom were the defendant's apprentices, and the defendant also worshiped He Qing'en as his master. After verifying the confessions, Judge Wu Tingqi ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody and adjourned the hearing to the 14th.

A Bloody Ear 167

Pirates Kidnap People for Ransom as a Show of Force

5,000 Yuan Must be Sent Within Three Days

The previous reports had described that Fengli Town, outside Wusongkou, was occupied by pirates. It is now learned that the pirate gang, after being suppressed by the police, fled in their entirety. It is reported that at around 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, a large gang of pirates returned, numbering over a thousand, which was even more rampant than before. There were more than 40 pirate ships, which were moored at various ports such as Yangbeigang and Shayuwa, and guarded a small area. The pirates landed with weapons, including hand-held machine guns, and occupied civilian houses along the coast, extorting food. Residents fled in droves. The previously kidnapped farmer, Sang Shoutai, was demanded a price of 15,000 yuan. The family had already collected 10,000 yuan and sent it. The pirates were still not satisfied and sent a letter to Sang's family, along with a bloody ear, to show their intent to receive a reply. They gave a deadline of three days to send the remaining 5,000 yuan, or they would tear up the ticket.

The Circumstances of the Death of a Water Police Detective in the Line of Duty 168

Repeatedly Solving Major Cases, Tragically Meeting an Untimely End

The Corpse's Wife Came to Shanghai Yesterday to Claim the Body

Sun Huanwen, a native of Songjiang, who was a detective of the First Squad of the First District of the Jiangsu Water Police and also an inspector of the Zhejiang Water Police, was assassinated in Baoyu Lane in the French Concession the night before last. It was reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that Sun captured Tai Bao Ashu's younger brother, nicknamed San Lao Ban, the leader of the Taihu bandits, in Shanghai last month and sent him to the Zhejiang government for interrogation. He confessed that the bandit gang was scattered in Shanghai. The superior sent Sun to Shanghai to arrest them. Sun knew that the bandit gang had many members and were very fierce, and it was difficult to arrest them. Therefore, he declared to the superior that he would sign a life-and-death contract. If he encountered an accident while arresting bandits, the government should generously compensate his family. With the permission of the superior, he brought his documents and colleagues to Shanghai a few days ago, staying in a hotel to investigate and arrest the bandits. The night before last, Sun and his colleagues and friends went to a friend's house upstairs at No. 10, Alley 1, Baoyu Lane, French Concession to meet and smoke. At 9:30 PM, they suddenly heard someone calling downstairs. Sun immediately went downstairs alone. When he reached the foot of the staircase, he was suddenly rushed out by the bandit gang, who fired several shots at Sun, hitting him four times in the groin, wrist, and other places. The murderers, seeing that their goal had been achieved, fled outwards in a crowd. At that time, Sun, still wounded, went upstairs. Later, his friends hired a car to take him to Renji Hospital for treatment. When he entered the hospital, he could still speak. The hospital reported to the police station, who sent detectives to investigate the scene of the incident. At the same time, the doctor performed an operation to remove two bullets, applied medicine, and bandaged the wound. Unfortunately, the injuries were too severe, and the treatment was ineffective. He died soon after. The hospital notified the police station, who sent detectives to notify the Tongren Fuyuantang funeral home, who sent a coffin carrier to bring the body to the mortuary at 7:30 AM yesterday. At the same time, the friends of the deceased sent people to Songjiang to urge the corpse's wife, Gu, to bring her children to Shanghai to report to the police station. Then, the Criminal Section reported to the French Court's Judge Zhu at 2:00 PM to examine the corpse and take a statement, sat at the judge's seat to examine the

Page 16

Fourth Sheet 169

case. According to the Bao Detective's report of the case, after Mr. Zhu questioned the deceased's friend, Weng Yousong, as a witness, he ordered the police station to take photos of the corpse and allow the family to prepare a coffin and collect the body themselves, and to wait for the arrest of the murderer. The deceased was quite capable in his work before his death, repeatedly solving major cases and earning the praise of his superiors. Also, at that time, a certain woman surnamed Mou happened to be passing by the staircase, and the cape she was wearing was pierced by a stray bullet.

Aftermath of the Zhabei Military Clothing Factory Fire 170

A Total of Two Women Have Died So Far

The Perpetrator is Still in Custody

At 5:30 PM the day before yesterday, a fire broke out suddenly at the Rongchangxiang military uniform temporary workshop on Tiande Road, Hujia Muqiao, Zhabei. The details have been reported in yesterday's newspapers. The following is a continuation of the investigation:

The Loss is Relatively Small: The management of the factory has always been strict, and smoking is prohibited in the workshop. Unexpectedly, a worker, Mao Yongshi, violated the prohibition and secretly smoked, causing a major disaster. However, two days ago, the factory still had thousands of sets of various military uniforms that had just been completed, and there were more than 600 workers. By the night before last, everything had been completed, leaving only 300 workers and over 600 sets of military uniforms. Although it was unfortunate to suffer a disaster, fortunately it happened two days later, so the loss was only in the range of four to five thousand yuan. Also, because the reed shed fence had doors on all sides, the workers were able to escape in all directions during the incident, which was not as devastating as the loss of the Fuchang military uniform factory a few days ago. It was also a great stroke of luck in the misfortune.

Two Women Died Tragically: The female worker Qin Liu's tragic death was not because she could not escape, but because she fell outside the factory in the panic and was trampled to death, which is very pitiful. Yesterday morning, the family of the deceased requested the court to waive the examination, and the factory provided generous compensation, which the family of the deceased received to take care of the aftermath. Another person who was burned, Jiang Zhang, died in the hospital yesterday after being sent to Jisheng Hospital on Baoshan Road by the Zhabei Third Fire Brigade. Jiang Zhang was 48 years old, from Yancheng, and lived on a boat in the Houhebang of Taiping Lane, Taiping Bridge.

How many straw sheds built by poor people from Jiangbei behind the factory were burned down is currently being thoroughly investigated by the Public Security Bureau. Once detailed household names are obtained, the factory intends to provide appropriate compensation.

The Workers Who Caused the Disaster: Ni Zhongmei, Chen Yicheng, and Cao Songquan, the three who were detained after causing the disaster, have been released on bail after being questioned by the Public Security Bureau. However, Mao Yongshi, as the person who started the fire, should be held responsible for the punishment and is still in custody, awaiting review by the court.

A Man Throws Himself into the Huangpu River 172

Claiming to Fear False Accusations by Kidnappers

His Nerves Seem to Have Suffered a Major Stimulus

At 7:00 AM yesterday, a man over forty years old hailed a sampan No. 1004 at the Nanjing Road Wharf, saying he was going to Pudong. Unexpectedly, when the sampan reached the center of the river, the man suddenly jumped into the Huangpu River to commit suicide without saying a word. The sampan man struggled to rescue him. Before long, he jumped into the river again to commit suicide, but was still rescued. Because there was not much water, there was no danger to his life. The sampan man Xu Genfu sent him to the Water Police Station. First, Xu described the passenger's two attempts to throw himself into the river. When questioned, the man said his name was Yu Xinghai, 45 years old, from Henan, and lived in the home of Liu Yongfu, a detective, near the Hanqiao in Zhabei. Because the kidnapper Liu Renrong had a grudge against him, and Liu Renrong was arrested and prosecuted for committing a crime two months ago, he was afraid that he would be falsely accused, so he sought this short-sighted end. When asked where Liu Renrong had committed the crime and where he was being held, he replied that he did not know at all. When asked how many people were in his family, he replied only three, but he could not say who the three were. After a while, he muttered to himself, and his condition was like madness. The police chief, considering that his words were incoherent and his nerves seemed to have suffered a major stimulus, ordered Detective Wu Rongsheng to escort him to the District Court for disposal.

The Sentence in the Case of a Mother Killing Her Child 178

The Original Sentence Was Revoked

Reduced to Three Months' Imprisonment

Later, because Jishun died, he went on to sue for causing death by injury. The first instance sentenced Chen Yinbao to three years and six months in prison for abandonment. Chen was not satisfied and appealed, still hiring lawyer Qu Yue to defend her, strongly arguing that the original sentence of abandonment was untenable. Yesterday, Shen Tingzhang, the president of the Jiangsu High Court, presided over the pronouncement of the sentence, the main points of which were: the original judgment was revoked, Chen Yinbao had no intention of killing, but the act of causing harm to a person was sentenced to three months' imprisonment, and the number of days of pre-trial detention were converted to one day of imprisonment for every two days.

Li Yuankang, Who Sells Counterfeit Trademark Cigarettes, Has Been Arrested 179

Sentenced to Three Months' Imprisonment and Fined 400 Yuan

Li Yuankang, a shareholder of the Japanese Hongfu Tobacco Company on Qipu Road and a native of Ningbo, colluded with his fellow villager Yu Bingyang, who had already been punished, on October 16th at around 8:00 PM to mix and sell counterfeit cigarettes, disguised as the Qimei brand cigarettes produced by the Chinese Xinglong Tobacco Company on North Henan Road, in two boxes, totaling 100,000 cigarettes, to the Tongqing Cigarette Paper Shop on Tongyun Street in the French Concession. He fled after the incident. Delong Tobacco Company offered a reward of 200 yuan in the newspaper for his arrest. The day before yesterday at noon, detectives Liu Junjie and Western Detective Clark of the Hongkou Police Station learned that Li Yuankang was sipping tea in the Leyuan Tea Shop at No. 2, Ximen Road in the French Concession. They then secretly went to the address with detectives from the French Police Station and arrested Li and brought him back to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the Special District Court. The police station's lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated the facts of the case and said that the defendant was indeed the principal offender, and requested severe punishment. When questioned, the defendant confessed that the counterfeit brand cigarettes were sold to him by Zhang A'de, who was on the run, saying that they were goods confiscated by the tax bureau, but he did not know the truth. The rest of his confession was evasive. The representative of Delong Tobacco Company, lawyer Huang Yuping, stated that the goods confiscated by the tax bureau did not have stamps and were stamped with the tax bureau's seal. The defendant was an expert in cigarettes, so how could he not know? Therefore, he requested the court's attention. After the court hearing, Judge Feng Shide sentenced Li Yuankang to three months' imprisonment and a fine of 400 yuan for selling cigarettes with counterfeit trademarks. If the fine was converted to imprisonment, two yuan would be deducted for each day. The number of days of pre-trial detention were converted to one day of imprisonment for every two days.

Negligence at the Pauper Asylum Leads to False Alarm 180

Police Force Scrambles in Vain

The Shanghai Charity Organization established this pauper asylum behind the Second Prison in Caohejing. The number of inmates has reached over 450. Under the meticulous planning and reorganization by Director Wu Tang, it has achieved considerable success. Due to a riot that occurred in the asylum in August last year, an alarm bell was installed at that time, connected to the Sixth District, Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau, and the Caohejing District Security Corps, so that in the event of an accident, they could be immediately notified to suppress it. Unexpectedly, the other day, the asylum needed to add an alarm bell in the dining hall. An electrical worker accidentally cut the wrong wire, causing the alarm bell to be triggered, ringing non-stop for a while. Forty or fifty people from the Public Security Bureau's police brigade and the Security Corps, all fully armed, rushed to the asylum. The neighbors were shocked and did not know what to do. After learning that no incident had occurred, they all regrouped and left. Afterwards, Director Wu went to various agencies to explain and apologize, and sent letters to the Public Security Bureau and the Security Corps, thanking them for their courage in their duties.

Jiangbei Notorious Bandit Leader Guan Huang Zaisong Captured 181

Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, the Fourth Patrol Team of the Wusong Public Security Bureau received a tip-off that two notorious bandits from Jiangbei were hiding inside the Jinlitai, a three-masted Chaohu sand barge moored at Dongpubin. The team immediately dispatched Patrol Leader Wang Songshan, along with patrolmen Wang Xingqi, Xiao Jiasheng, Zhu Shukuai, and others, all fully armed, to board the ship. They captured the two bandits, Guan Biaolin and Huang Tian. They also found two new large leather suitcases and a rattan basket belonging to the bandits, containing a large number of silk fabric clothes. Patrol Leader Wang brought the bandits to the team headquarters. After a brief interrogation by Team Leader Bai, due to the involvement of notorious bandits, police were dispatched to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for further investigation. The Jinlitai sand barge and its crew were detained pending orders for investigation. According to the reporter, Wang Weizhong, from Guanyun County, Jiangbei, the two bandits have been bandits since 1927. On June 17, 1928, Guan Biaolin led dozens of bandits into Wang Weizhong's home, intending to rob and kill. Wang cleverly hid and was unharmed. The bandits killed Wang's steward, Wang Dafu, and kidnapped Cai Hengshan, leaving no remains. The situation was very cruel. Wang Dafu's son sued the Guanyun County government, ordering a wanted notice. They were later arrested in Yangkou, Shuyang, and handed over to Guanyun County by the Xiangshuikou Joint Defense Association. Due to the bandits' cunning confessions, it was difficult to make a judgment. On the seventh day of the first lunar month of this year, the bandits escaped from prison, taking away 43 other important criminals. The Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Department of Civil Affairs have issued wanted notices. After their escape, the bandits hid in places like Sanjiaozhen and Lvsi, specializing in kidnapping and robbery. Later, they joined Ma Yuren's forces and served in the rear army. After Ma Yuren failed in Yancheng, the bandits hid in Shanghai, intending to return to Jiangbei to become bandits again. Unexpectedly, the long arm of the law caught them when they were spotted and arrested.

House Construction Lawsuit Settled Out of Court 185

Shen Xingtao, the owner of Shen Xingji, located at 1270 Lafayette Road in the French Concession, and a native of Pudong, previously contracted to build several houses at the intersection of Qipu Road and Rehe Road. The agreed price was 11,700 taels. After completion, the owner, Han Qixiang, needed additional renovations, which Shen carried out, costing a total of over 1,533 taels. Han delayed payment for this amount, only giving Shen Xiang 250 yuan. Shen hired lawyer Yan Luqing to sue Han in the Special District Court. Han also sued Shen in the French Mixed Court for cutting corners and using inferior materials. Yesterday morning, the Special Court summoned Shen for the case of Shen suing Han. Lawyer Yan requested that the court first rule on whether the court should accept the case, stating that the French Mixed Court was not a legally recognized court by the Chinese government and could not accept the case. The presiding judge, Zhou Daren, believed that the defendant's residence and the building's foundation were both in the Public Concession and should be accepted by the court, so he proceeded with the trial. The plaintiff stated that he had not received a penny for the additional work, except for the 250 yuan. The defendant's lawyer stated that payment had already been made and presented a receipt as evidence. Judge Zhou believed that proceeding with the case would be detrimental to both parties and suggested settling out of court. He adjourned the case for a later hearing.

Detective Arrests a Robber 186

While Zhengmeiyu Cigarette Paper Shop at 701 Zhejiang Road was sorting out loose change at 10:40 PM the night before last, two robbers suddenly reached into the counter and stole more than 30 pieces of change and fled. Zhou Changlin, a shop assistant, chased after them to Fuzhou Road, where Cui Chengke, a Chinese detective from the Lao Zha Police Station, and Chinese police officer No. 2217 were patrolling. They stopped one of the robbers and found a pistol, four bullets, and the stolen goods on him. He was taken to the police station. He identified himself as Yang Shaoqing, from Zhenjiang, and had previously served as a squad leader in the Seventh Division of the National Army. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the First Criminal Court of the Special Court. The police station's lawyer, Ru Baoqi, presented the case and stated that the police station's investigation procedures were not yet complete and requested a postponement. The plaintiff then testified about the robbery. The defendant confessed to the robbery but claimed to have been fooled by others. Presiding Judge Zhou Han ordered him to be detained pending a further hearing.

Liu Guangrong Abducts Xu Xishi 187

Liu Guangrong, a native of Nanjing, previously abducted Xu Xishi (30 years old) from Wuhu to Shanghai under the pretext of recommending her as a domestic helper. He arranged for her to marry Ma Renke, who lived at 266 Xinjiang Road, Zhabei, stating that the betrothal gift was 60 yuan. After she married, Ma did not pay the betrothal gift. Liu went to collect the money but was unsuccessful. He wrote to Wuhu and brought Xu's husband to Shanghai to negotiate with Ma. The day before yesterday, Ma twisted Liu Guangrong and accused him to the First Branch of the Fourth District. After questioning by the station chief, Liu was detained for abducting a married woman with the intention of profiting. Yesterday, he was formally submitted to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation.

News from the Silk Industry Public Bond Negotiations 188

Due to the increasing stagnation of silk sales in Europe and America, silk factories in Shanghai have suffered heavy losses and are unable to sustain themselves. By the end of last month, all 106 silk factories in Shanghai had suspended operations, awaiting government relief. Representatives from the silk factories in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai, including Shen Huachen, have gone to Beijing to petition the government. Yesterday, a telegram from Beijing stated that the nine representatives met with Song and Kong, heads of the Executive Yuan's Ministry of Finance and Ministry of Industry and Commerce, respectively, and presented the critical situation of the silk industry. They requested that the government issue 10 million yuan in silk industry public bonds within the year to provide relief. Song and Kong both expressed their acceptance, but the approval will take time, and it will be difficult for the silk factories to resume operations immediately.

Weather Report 193

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Yangtze River Basin and the Shandong coast are cloudy and changing, due to a low pressure in Mongolia moving towards the southeast-east. There is a southwest wind north of Shandong. The wind over the Yellow Sea and the East China Sea is from the northwest to the northeast. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this area was 56.5 degrees and the lowest was 34.2 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 65.7 degrees and the lowest was 54.5 degrees.

Special Feature

Retrospect and Prospect of the Chinese Child Welfare Association (Continued) by Wu Weide 194

Since the establishment of our association, we have been fortunate to receive the support of virtuous and talented individuals in the country, who are willing to sacrifice their time, energy, and money, and contribute their knowledge, talents, and experience to serve our association. This is something we deeply admire and are extremely grateful for. Although they do not need our admiration and gratitude, those who are now willing to fulfill their obligations and serve on various committees of our association include: Executive Committee members Minister Kong Yongzhi, Luo Yunyan, Mrs. Guo Bingwen, Mr. Gao Fengchi, Mr. Li Daonan, Professor Chen Heqin, Ms. Ding Shujing, Judge Hu Yigu, Dr. Yu Rizhang, Dr. Cheng Jingyi, Mrs. Liu Zhanen, Mrs. Fu Bulan, Dr. Hu Xuanming, Dr. Niu Huisheng, Dr. Le Lingsheng, Dr. Fei Peide, and Dr. Kuang Fuzhuo. Others include Mr. Zhu Chengzhang, Mr. Fei Wusheng, Mr. Huang Jingwan, Mr. Niu Huiling, Mrs. Guo Biao, Diao Defu, Mrs. Anderson, Mrs. Guo Shun, Ms. Zhang Zhenduo, Dr. Fu Wenshou, Dr. Shi Meiyu, Dr. Huang Bingji, Dr. Wang Shuzhen, Ms. Yin Cuihe, Mr. Fu Ruoyu, Dr. Wang Zonghai, Dr. Fan Dingjiu, Mr. Feng Zikai, Dr. Sun Keji, Mrs. Wu Weide, Ms. Guan Cuizhen, Dr. Lin Yutang, Mr. Powell, and Ms. Li Guanfang. They all have extremely busy jobs and extremely heavy workloads, yet they are willing to take time out of their precious free time to serve our association. This is truly commendable and naturally admirable. If not for their enthusiasm for promoting the happiness of children, how could they achieve this? As the saying goes, "Who can surpass me in loving goodness?" I think there will be many in the country who will rise up in response to this call.

Exerting a bit of effort yields a bit of results. We only fear that we do not strive now, how can we expect success in the future? When we look at the past, our hearts are filled with a myriad of thoughts. On the one hand, in addition to considerable satisfaction, we are even more self-motivated. On the other hand, in addition to constantly admonishing ourselves, we also feel the necessity of expanding our organization, increasing our strength, and uniting more comrades to strive forward with us for the child welfare movement. With the calls and efforts of a few people, we have managed to achieve today's insignificant results. If we can gather the backbone of the entire country, stand on the same battle line, and work together for the goal of child welfare, then wouldn't the achievements that may be manifested in the future be even more brilliant and splendid? Wouldn't the happiness of Chinese children be even more fulfilling and complete? Wouldn't the strength of the Chinese nation be even more robust and increased? Wouldn't the foundation of the Chinese nation be even more solid and stable? As the saying goes, "Many hands make light work" and "United we stand." These are truly unbreakable famous sayings. The meaning of our enthusiastic solicitation of members this time lies in this.

The child welfare movement is a movement to plant a permanent plan for our nation, a movement to seek fundamental construction for our country. Since we are part of the Chinese nation and have a considerable responsibility for the construction of the Chinese nation, then in the face of this great movement, how can we stand idly by like Qin Yueren, who saw the leanness and fatness of others without telling them? We should bravely and resolutely join in cooperation to promote its success. Dr. Wang Zhengting said it well: "The happiness of children is the foundation of the happiness of the people of the whole country. The work of the Chinese Child Welfare Association is something that all Chinese people should enthusiastically support and vigorously assist." I hope my compatriots will repeatedly reflect on these words. "The future is long" and "the responsibility is heavy." The cause of child welfare is by no means comparable to trivial matters. The purpose of our association is to seek happiness for the children of the entire China. If any child is still mired in the sea of suffering, still struggling in adversity and displacement, then it shows that the responsibility of our association has not ended and the work of our association has not been completed and we still need to continue our efforts. We have no time to rest, how can we slightly harbor the thought of leisure? Friends, this cold reality is too far from our ideals. We should build solid camps and fight to the death, stand on the same battle line, and strive forward together! Promote the happiness of children and complete the child welfare movement. Gentlemen with aspirations, why don't you rise up and come?

Letter to the Editor 195

Esteemed Mr. Editor,

I have read your esteemed newspaper's report about the accidental mistake of Hui Luo Company, which stated that Xin Yi Construction Company used a platform as a workshop, with a small platform more than ten feet high built in the center to place a pot for boiling asphalt. This does not correspond to the facts. Our company is responsible for the asphalt project and has never built a high platform. Moreover, the place where the pot is placed is the lowest part of the star surface, and our workers have not yet started work. How could there be a source of fire? I am afraid that the error will be transmitted by mistake. Here are the real circumstances. I hope that you will correct it so that all parties will know the truth. I am deeply grateful. I wish you good health.

Sincerely,

Anmei Foreign Firm

November 5, 1920

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter 196

— Hai Ke

Guest (running to the hotel bookkeeper in the middle of the night) — Mr. Bookkeeper, I want to change rooms.

Bookkeeper — Why change rooms? You can do it tomorrow.

Guest — No, I need to change immediately.

Bookkeeper — This is not the time to change rooms. Let's talk about it tomorrow morning.

Guest — It must be changed, or I'm leaving immediately.

Bookkeeper — Then what is the reason?

Guest — Because the room I'm staying in is on fire!

Husband — Darling, Mr. C passed away last night, leaving behind one million dollars. If you became his widow, you could enjoy it for the rest of your life.

Wife — I don't care about that. I love you. I only want to be your widow.

Housewife (asking the maid) — Wang Ma, did you see a basket of eggs on the kitchen floor?

Maid — I didn't see it, but it seems like I stepped on something.

Teacher (to the students) — Here are two rich men. One became rich through legitimate business, and the other became rich by swindling others. Which one do you want to be?

A student — Teacher, I don't care about anything else. I just want to know which one makes more money.

Man — My love, have you always had these headaches?

Woman — No, only since I became your lover.

Tidbits from the Political Scene 197

— UB

Anyone with a slight knowledge of the capital knows of Cao the cook. Cao was the chef of former Premier Tan Zukong's household for generations. Throughout his life, Mr. Tan abstained from the temptations of pleasure, women, and wealth. However, he had a fondness for rich and fresh delicacies, and would not enjoy his meals unless they were prepared by Cao. Guests who wanted to feast with Mr. Tan would first hire Cao to prepare a shark fin banquet, typically rewarding him with one hundred and fifty gold pieces. Therefore, there were few important figures in the political scene who did not know Cao the cook.

Mr. Tan would always bring Cao the cook with him whenever he traveled to Shanghai. One evening, Major He planned to take the night train from Shanghai to Nanjing back to Beijing. When he arrived at the station, it was already late. He asked a station clerk and learned that the berths were sold out. Only in the adjutant's compartment of Premier Tan, there was still a way to arrange a berth. Thinking that it was the adjutant of Premier Tan, maybe he was familiar with him, so He hurried on the train. When he opened the door, he was shocked to see it was Cao the cook.

The Tan family had strict rules, and Cao the cook also acted prudently and adhered to the rules. Throughout Mr. Tan's life, Cao the cook never dared to overstep the boundaries. It can be seen that a famous figure of a generation has his own true nature. After Mr. Tan's death, Cao mourned him with a couplet: "Serving and pleasing, I remember those years. When the young master walked in the courtyard, I also shared the joys and hardships. Governing the country and cooking are not easy tasks. Now that the master is gone, who understands the heart of harmonizing the cauldron?"

After Mr. Tan's death, the mourning couplets and sacrificial banners presented by various sectors were dazzling and beautiful. There were still undiscovered treasures from overseas that were not hung out that day. The upper inscription read "Old Brother Zu'an, May You Rest in Peace," and the lower inscription boldly read "From Your Brother Wu Peifu." The couplet read: "The road to Shu is difficult, and the apes of the Wu Gorge weep with lines of tears. Changsha mourns, and the wild geese of Hengyang carry several letters." The feelings are evident in the words, and Wu Peifu is the most heartbroken person today.

A Hundred-Year-Old Brandy in the Family 198

— Li Qingduo

"How can I obtain Zhongshan's thousand-day wine, and become intoxicated until the time of peace?" This is a poem by Wang Zhong of the Song Dynasty. In recent years, wars have been frequent, and we today have this thought. The first line is suitable for us to chant. In the poems of the past, there were many who chanted about wine, and there were many who were good drinkers. It can be seen that pure mellow wine is favored by many refined scholars and poets. Therefore, I will occasionally write about wine. Wine is best when it is old. Those who are good at drinking or those who love antiquity often have precious collections. Mr. Chen Huanzhi, a wealthy businessman in Shanghai, likes to play with antiques. He has several bottles of brandy in his family, made in France. The year of manufacture was 1830 AD. Mr. Chen has been collecting it for seventy years. This year is 1930 AD. The wine has been around for a hundred years. It can be called old. The aroma is refreshing and unusual. Mr. Chen cherishes it like a treasure and keeps it carefully. Recently, because there were friends who were good drinkers, he took out two bottles of this fine wine and gave them to his friends. The recipients were as if they had obtained a rare treasure, and they used it to entertain distinguished guests, who all appreciated it. For a time, it was spread as a good story.

The Great Decisive Battle of Yan Feng's Final Days 199

— Ji Ya

Since Yan Feng unleashed their troops and the central government issued an order to suppress them, they have been stalemated on the Jinpu, Longhai, and Pinghan lines for almost five or six months. Finally, the Battle of Xinzheng led to the collapse of Yan Feng. Although it can be said that the situations of obedience and rebellion were different, the spirit of the central generals who bravely advanced was enough to chill the enemy's courage and prevent them from being willing to fight. The great decisive battle of Yan Feng's final days will be recorded on the left, which will be appreciated by those who remained for this war.

The Situation Before the Decisive Battle: In late September, the Central Army, through its efforts, broke through the stalemate that had lasted for months. On the Longhai Line, they defeated the enemy west of Neihuang and Suixian. On the Pinghan Line, they defeated the enemy at Linying and Xuchang. After these disastrous defeats, Yan Feng concentrated their main forces on the Longhai Line near Kaifeng and Chenliu, and their main forces on the Pinghan Line near Changge and Xinzheng. They shortened the front line and connected the two routes, hoping to wait for work at leisure and make a final struggle.

The Six Divisions Marched Day and Night: At that time, the Central Army formed more than ten columns, taking advantage of the victory to drive straight to Zhengzhou and Luoyang, in order to cut off the enemy's retreat. The Sixth Division then followed up and pursued after defeating the main enemy forces near Suixian, and went straight to Qixian County. It was then incorporated into the Ninth Column, and together with the Ninth Division and the Fifty-third Division, turned to advance on the Pinghan Road. After passing through Tongxu, Fugou, Weishi, Yanling, and several other counties, they marched day and night, lightly armed and quickly. After seven days and nights, they gathered between Changge and Weichuan. The enemy had fortified defenses at every turn, and the fortifications were particularly strong. The Ninth Column, having been ordered to advance towards Zhengzhou, ventured in three routes, encountering enemy encirclements along the way, so as not to leak the news. Finally, on October 1, they seized the Xueji and Xuedian stations between Xinzheng and Zhengzhou. While removing the railway and telegraph wires to cut off transportation, the Sixth Division divided the 18th Brigade Chen Shiji's unit to cooperate with friendly forces to guard the north, and the main force of the 18th Brigade and the entire 17th Brigade turned south to attack the enemy's back. Fan Songfu approached Xinzheng on October 3.

Feng's Army Was Surrounded on All Sides: After October 2, the Central Army, sharpening their spirits, joined forces to attack fiercely. The enemy, such as Zhang Weixi, Zhao Fenglin, Ni Yusheng, Tian Jinkai, Wang Hemin, Feng Zhi'an, Deng Baoshan, Ren Yingqi and other units, no less than hundreds of thousands of people, were surrounded separately by the Central Army, so that they could not take care of each other and became turtles in a jar one by one. After three days and nights of fierce fighting, the enemy suffered countless casualties. Then Zhang Weixi sent an envoy to request a ceasefire, and was willing to send a telegram listing Feng Yuxiang's crimes and begging the central government to reorganize them. Zhao Guantao, the commander of the Sixth Division, believed that time should not be lost and the enemy should not be let go, and urgently asked Commander-in-Chief Chiang to thoroughly resolve the situation to avoid future troubles. At that time, Commander Gu, who commanded the siege of various divisions, also saw through his treachery. He replied to the envoy, "Hand over your guns before you open your mouth." The envoy left without understanding. Zhang Weixi, unable to do anything, convened a military conference. Just as they were sobbing and at a loss, large bombs from the Central Air Force planes were dropped one after another. For a time, all the participants fled in panic. In addition to the Ninth Column, the Central Army in this battle included the Eleventh, Sixtieth, Sixty-first, Second, Third, and Twenty-third Divisions.

Feng's Army Collapsed Completely: The enemy near Xinzheng had been surrounded separately by the Central Army, and the 18th Brigade Chen Shiji's unit of the Sixth Division surrounded Ni Yusheng's infantry brigade and Zhang Weixi's artillery regiment. Later, due to lack of food and reinforcements, they were willing to surrender unconditionally. More than 3,000 rifles, more than 30 artillery pieces, more than 400 mules and horses, and more than 4,000 officers and soldiers were all confiscated by the Sixth Division. The enemy army was greatly shocked, which led to the complete collapse on October 6. More than 20 senior military officers, including Zhang Weixi, were taken prisoner. Later, according to Commander-in-Chief Chiang's telegram, their lives were preserved and they were employed at discretion to give them a chance to reform. Middle and lower-level officers were sent to schools for training, and soldiers were sent back to their hometowns. The Yellow River and Luo River area was cleared.

Gleanings from the Second Anniversary of the Ministry of Railways 200

— Guqu Zhoulang

The Second Anniversary of the Ministry of Railways was held on November 1. There are two notable events that have not been seen in the newspapers.

1. The final magic trick. A person took the stage alone, holding an empty blanket. In an instant, he conjured up a large number of pre-mounted congratulatory couplets, as many as six or seven pairs, all with excellent writing. Unfortunately, the text was too long to remember. He conjured up a brocade banner of more than ten feet long, with the five golden characters "Complete 100,000 Miles" attached. The upper and lower inscriptions were complete, as a congratulation to the Ministry from all the staff. However, this section was not announced in advance, so the guests did not wait to watch it, which is a pity. The instructor claimed that the magician was "Wang Yang Dahai" (Vast Ocean), which was neither a name nor a nickname, which made people feel puzzled.

2. The enchanting dance and the decoration of the lounge, dazzling. Red men and green women, hugging each other in gorgeous costumes, dancing to the melodious music. It is indeed soul-stirring. Other performances, such as the new drama using Yang Sou, Zhang's wife, and the magistrate, and the hanging ghost, were the most wonderful. All seven old dramas were commendable, especially Tian Ba's Worshiping the Mountain was unique.

Eulogy to Mr. Tian of Qichun (Part 2) 201

— Loudong Feng Chao

Alas, when the People's Party was first established, it drove out the Manchus. Heroes from all directions, like rain and clouds, with articles and integrity, as beautiful as the sun and stars, achieved the success of the Xinhai Revolution. However, after the conquest of the wind, the customs of scholars became ambiguous, and those who upheld integrity either suffered wrongful executions, were imprisoned, fled to foreign lands, or buried themselves in desolate mountains. Therefore, Zifang had the tour of Chisong, and Shaobo had the boating on the Five Lakes. The world was turbid, floating in the dust, without gaining filth. Although poor, they did not regret it. When their hearts were depressed, they expressed it in articles, like Qu Yuan's "Li Sao" and Wen Shan's "Song of Righteousness," which were all works of talented people expressing their anger, enough to be immortalized in the future. As for you, sir, your late years were especially strong. Knowing that the world could not tolerate you, you wrote the Great Peace Plan, forming your own school of thought. Your arguments were like Jia Sheng's memorial on politics, and your literary talent was like Dong Zhongshu's response to the virtuous and talented. You melted the codes and systems of ancient and modern times, based on Sun Yat-sen's principles, and extracted the legal ideas of Europe and America, establishing a century-long plan and leaving a guideline for thousands of years. If Mr. Sun were here, he would not change these words. You once said to me, Chao, "What I have written, this is the most important. Sitting and talking about it can be put into practice. It is not the opinion of a scholar." Alas, your words are still in my ears. How can I not be sad? In ancient times, there were famous works written by fathers and narrated by sons, such as Zichang, Meng Jian, and Silian. Clearly displayed in the past, from now on, the unfinished business will be entrusted to Cui Ji to continue well. Chao is young and has no special expertise, but you alone thought he was teachable. As the saying goes, "To have one confidant is enough." If I had met you ten years ago, I could have followed you and served the Party and the country. Now I see you in your illness, unable to listen to your teachings, and you are gone. Thinking of you in the wind, the sorrow cannot be supported. Alas, woe is me, our lord, as incorruptible as Xu You, as detached as Zhuang Guang, as resolute as Tian Heng, as loyal as Wu Mu, as benevolent as Mo Di, as grand as Chen Liang. Your life should have been as long as that of Fenyang. Why did you abandon our Republic of China and pass away when you were over fifty, with your writings unfinished and your policies not implemented? People in the past have said, "Born to be a hero, die to be a spirit." May your spirit be as beautiful as the sun and moon, may your principles be glorious, shining as the stars, displaying the constitution, fighting as thunder, striking the jackals, stern as frost, encouraging our talented people, transforming into rain, nourishing all directions, turning into wind and clouds, awing all directions. It is your dead body, but your heroic spirit will be passed on forever. Alas, there is no greater sorrow than the death of a national scholar, and no greater pain than the loss of a confidant. The water of the Yangtze River flows forever. When will the sorrow in my heart end? Remembering your life, I write my sorrow and entanglement. May you appreciate my sincerity and come to receive it. Alas, woe is me.

Attached are the mourning couplets of Feng Ping (Xinxia) and Feng Xu Jingcun (Suhua):

Broad and profound, you are a great scholar; heroic and fierce, you are a great knight. Striving for revolution, you are a founding hero; your good policies are written too much, and you should cast a model for all time.

Your wisdom and strategy were in Hanyang; your righteousness and courage were on the Huai River. Your surprising victories were on the Yangtze River. Your famous name will last forever. I am ashamed to have no capable pen to record Tian Heng.

Mourning couplets of Feng Fei (Jinan) and Feng Jiao (Jiaoyue):

On the establishment of the capital, on the equalization of land use, on the governance of the Yellow River, matters concerning the national economy and the people's livelihood, you consulted ancient and modern times to create your own strategies.

You were a founding hero, a literary master, and a scholar. Now you have fallen and the trees have withered, weeping for the country and mourning for this person.

Warmth in the Heart (309) 202

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Fifteen: Tears Shed in All Directions, Red Love Sorrowful; Hearts Captivated in One Place, Green Meaning Lingering

For those who die suddenly of lung disease, there are two crucial points: twenty years old and thirty years old. The twenty-year-old mark is the most dangerous. Young people who get lung disease are often sixteen or seventeen, eighteen or nineteen. Their lungs are most tender and easily eroded. At the age of twenty, whether male or female, they are the objects of great hope from their parents, and they themselves have many good youths. They are just thinking of diligently studying and gradually reaching adulthood, but suddenly they die young. This is the most painful and regrettable thing. However, those who get lung disease during the developmental period often cannot escape this mark. Once this mark is passed, they must escape the second mark of thirty years old. This can be considered the next danger. During that period, there is also the issue of sexual desire, which often promotes the disease and makes it worse. If they can escape this mark, the danger will be greatly reduced. Therefore, there are often many people who, in their thirties, look like they will never live to be forty years old. But by their forties, they are still the same old consumptive ghost. By their fifties, they are still an often sickly old man. This is like a carrying pole. As the weight of age is added, you only see the pole bending, but it won't break for a while. Unfortunately, Liu Xingshu could not escape the second mark of thirty years old. When consumptive disease reached the point of being bedridden, people in Jiangsu and Zhejiang call it "consumptive disease in bed." When they are not in bed, they occasionally have attacks, but when they are not sick, they can still walk freely. Once they are in bed, it's over. The most distressing thing is that there is no way to save them. The doctor has already shaken his head and refused. The family members no longer hope that he will be reborn. Everyone knows he is going to die. They just hide it from the patient himself, telling him comforting words. This is even harder than announcing a death sentence. You must know that prisoners who are sentenced to death still have hope of being pardoned before the execution, and they still have hope of having their cases overturned. But where can this death sentence on the sick body go to find the master of nature to beg for leniency and ask him to postpone it for a moment? But how can people endure this time of waiting for death? Zuo Shichen had visited Liu Xingshu several times during his illness. The first time was when he was vomiting the most severely and had no strength to speak. Zuo Shichen didn't dare to talk to him much and left in a few minutes. The second time, he heard that the dangerous period had passed, and he desperately wanted a friend to talk to him. When he went to see him at that time, his body was so thin in the quilt that it was as flat as the body. When he stretched out his hand, it was like a bird's claw. When he saw Zuo Shichen, he cried miserably and said, "Old friend, I may not be able to see you again." Zuo Shichen could only comfort him and say that he could gradually get better in the future. He also thought that the dangerous period had passed. Probably patients often comfort themselves. In fact, the disease had already penetrated the bone marrow.

The cotton yarn market is increasingly sluggish. The appetite of various groups is weak, actual sales are disappointing, and the support from overseas markets is minimal. This situation has led to a difficult-to-reverse situation, and a new low price of 145 taels has been seen. The reporter has repeatedly mentioned this situation before. The only hope for the yarn market lies in actual sales and foreign markets. Now that the war is over, there is still no hope for prosperous sales. It is the season for a cold winter market, and the trend of overseas markets is generally sluggish. The protection of buyers has been lost, and there are already those who are gradually selling off. The atmosphere of weakness has enveloped the entire market, and the call for 42 or 43 taels is again prevalent. If there is no active development in actual sales, and the overseas market situation remains weak, it is not an exaggeration.
