Cotton Market Sluggish 209

The cotton market is sluggish due to the weakness of the yarn market, with new low prices appearing frequently, and actual sales are completely stagnant. The market atmosphere is desolate and lifeless, and the market situation is deteriorating. Manufacturers have a relatively large inventory and are less concerned, and imported cotton is continuously arriving. According to reports, Shanghai imported 27,678 bales of Indian cotton in September and 2,431 bales of American cotton. In November, 40,590 bales of Indian cotton and 31,560 bales of American cotton were imported. The comparison between September and October shows a rapid increase. Based on past situations, it is feared that the number of imports will increase even more in the future. The huge amount of foreign cotton imported is enough to put pressure on Chinese cotton. One reason is that the harvest is relatively poor, and they are unwilling to sell at low prices. Another reason is that inland transportation is blocked, transportation is inconvenient, and the market supply is scarce. Foreign cotton is repeatedly depreciated and sold, resulting in a huge amount of absorption. Given the sluggish appearance of the yarn market, and its tendency to further decline, it will be difficult to expect active transactions in the near future. The trend of foreign cotton is also unable to provide assistance. However, the calmness of the inland groups may temporarily lead to a fluctuating and sluggish situation.

The Cotton Market Follows the Yarn Market Exchange Han Standard, with Indian and English cotton falling, and the yarn market also declining. Bulls are gradually liquidating their positions, and the market atmosphere is very weak. However, the Han groups remain stable, with each month falling by 0.05 to 0.15 yuan. The market continued to decline in the afternoon, with each month continuing to fall by 0.05 to 0.1 yuan. The total transaction volume is 40,900 piculs.

Flour Market Mills Dump and Soften 212

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the market prices for various months were only slightly lower by about 0.2 yuan due to foreign imports. Because the competition between the long and short sides was very fierce, both inside and outside the industry could not help but wait and see, so transactions were very thin. At times, there was a slight uptick. Until the opening of the market in the afternoon, it was initially stable. Then, Fuxin and small and medium-sized mills continued to release large amounts of near and distant contracts, causing the entire market sentiment to be shaken. The prices for various months fell like a leaf swept away by a strong wind. The reason for this dumping is that the mills may have no hope for future actual sales, so they are dumping all their holdings, intending to go short. According to general predictions, a price of 1.5 yuan is already within sight, without any doubt. If the mills continue to dump, it would not be surprising if the price fell to 1 yuan. As a result, the current month fell by 0.2 fen compared to the previous day, December fell by 0.0325 yuan, January fell by 0.03 yuan, February fell by 0.0275 yuan, March fell by 0.035 yuan, and April fell by 0.0325 yuan.

Wheat Market Starts Weak, Ends Strong 213

Yesterday, the wheat market showed a pattern of initial weakness followed by firmness in the morning and afternoon. Initially, the market sentiment was still flat because foreign wheat was still only slightly lower by two or three jiao. Then, large short-selling accounts urgently covered their positions, so even though the flour market fell sharply and foreign wheat recovered slightly, the market atmosphere turned profitable. However, since the environment has not changed and the flour market continues to fall sharply, it is feared that the future will still be a decline. As a result, the current month was better by 0.03 yuan compared to the previous day, December was better by 0.1 yuan, January was unchanged, February and March were better by 0.1 yuan, and April was better by 0.4 yuan. The spot wheat market was still quiet throughout the city. Large factories still mutually excluded each other and did not trade. Only 500 bags of Yaowan wheat were opened at 4.3 yuan, and were purchased by Shen Da.

Ke Xian Rice Has Purchases on This Street 214

Yesterday, in the Ke Xian rice market, in addition to the Fujian group continuing to load and handle, this street also began to purchase. The source of supply was still small, and the inventory was not large. Therefore, the market situation immediately became tense. Jiangxi Ji Zao Gao rice opened again to 11 yuan, and medium-quality grades also rose, rising by 0.3 to 0.2 yuan compared to the previous day's market price. If this street continues to purchase in the future, the Fuzhou and Xiamen groups will not be able to press down prices as they did in the past, and the market can gradually turn around. The total transaction volume was 2,000 bags of Jiangxi Ji Zao rice, priced at 11 yuan, 11.078 yuan, and the next grade at 10.03 yuan. In addition, 250 bags of Zhong Guan Ji Wan rice were priced at 11.59 yuan, and 2 small carts of Nanjing Ji rice were priced at 9.45 to 9.2 yuan, which also saw an increase compared to the previous market.

Dried Goods Production of Honey Dates Decreases 215

Market Prices Tighten Daily

The current stock of honey dates is scarce, and market prices are tightening daily. This year's output is less than last year, and those in the area who engage in this business are all cautious. Most of them suffered losses last year, and more than half of them have stopped this year. Therefore, the goods currently shipped to Shanghai will not be loaded again until 60-70% of them have been sold, fearing that they will repeat the same mistakes. Due to this reason, the stock of goods is decreasing daily, and market prices are able to remain firm and trend higher. Recently, the buying appetite of the Guangdong group has been better, followed by this street, which is also considerable. Top-quality Hui Gong Chao Dan is sold for 31-32 taels, Hui Gong Tu Tu for 28 taels, and Lanxi Tu Tu for 24 taels. Upper and lower grades are added or reduced as usual.

New Lu Bamboo Shoots First Batch Has Opened 216

According to Min news, the output of new Lu bamboo shoots is quite large. However, due to bandit disturbances in that area, local unrest has led to delays in the arrival of goods. The arrival of goods has recently increased, and sales areas everywhere are mostly shipping out after listening to prices. However, because the National Lunar New Year is approaching, the pricing of various industries has already been opened. It is faintly heard that the industry considers the price too high, and the stock in the production area is quite large, so the intention to import is very weak. Customers still want to raise prices, resulting in not much arrival of goods daily. Compared with the spring market, it has already risen by two or three taels. Please refer to the price list for the prices of various varieties.

Sichuan Pickled Mustard Tuber Market Prices Loosen 217

There have been no new arrivals of Sichuan pickled mustard tuber recently. The current stock in the market is about 3,000, and it is gradually being released. The price of the top grade is 35 yuan, and the price of the next grade is one or two yuan less, which is looser than before. In terms of sales, although North Road, the inland, and this street are buying, the quantities are not smooth. The market price yesterday was 34 yuan for the top grade and 31-32 yuan for the ordinary grade. The market situation was flat.

Sugar Market Dumping Raw Sugar White Prices Should Be Rare 218

Spot Sugar Market May Decline

Yesterday, the sugar market production area telegrams stated that Cuban spot sugar and New York sugar futures had not arrived on the market. The price of Javanese spot sugar was 8.375, and the price of November and December futures was 8.125. Compared with the previous telegram, there was no increase or decrease. The Association market划盘 (hua pan) Dutch sugar No. 20, the buying interest in raw sugar white was depressed, and the export was quite large. The transaction price was 7 taels and 8.5 qian. The newly arrived goods that could not be exported were 7 taels and 8 qian, and the import and export were very slack. Milled fine sugar white was 7 taels and 9 qian, No. 20 medium sugar white was 6 taels and 9 qian, and inquiries were also few. No. 8 Dutch red was 6 taels and 3.5 qian, and the market was firmer. Transactions in Japanese sugar were also very sparse, and the market also declined. N mark was 7 taels and 7.5 qian, J mark was 8 taels and 0.075 qian, YRO mark was 7 taels and 3.25 qian, YT mark was 7 taels and 6.5 qian, and YR mark was 7 taels and 9.25 qian, which was a decline of 0.025 to 0.05 yuan compared to the previous day. The market atmosphere still showed signs of decline. Taikoo车糖 (che tang) R mark, delivery in February, was sold at a discount for 6 taels and 5 qian, the standard加税划划 (jia shui hua hua) price was 8 taels, and there were no takers. Dumping Dutch sugar raw sugar white also turned cheaper, and the discounted price was 5.95 yuan in Dutch currency. The industry's intention to import was weak, so it was also being delivered for the time being.

Metals Transactions Are Slack During the Autumn Races 219

Metal transactions have been slack in the past few days due to the Autumn Races. Because foreign firms only trade for half a day, buying and selling is exceptionally quiet. The standards for each item are unchanged because imports and exports are fresh, so there is no rise or fall. However, it is heard that among the new iron products, such as new foreign yuan, foreign plates, and triangular iron, the overseas pricing is trending weaker, so there are signs of relaxation.

Exports of Native Nails Are Very Active 220

Exports of native nails have been very active recently. There have been large-scale exports to Tianjin, Hankou, and other areas in recent days, and groups from Fujian, Shantou, and other places have also come to negotiate recently. Therefore, the number of nail exports yesterday was more than a thousand barrels. However, the market price has not changed.

Hui Si Iron Raises by 0.025 Yuan 221

Transactions of Hui Si iron have recently shown the vigor of spring grass after rain. Can factories, tobacco companies, and lard factories have all placed orders, so more than 2,000 boxes have been sold in the past two days. However, since the market goods have been purchased, they have become very scarce. Therefore, market prices are rising steadily. Yesterday, the price rose by another 0.025 yuan. The old steel mill is estimated at 22.5 taels, the new steel mill at 21.5 taels, and the Mitsui goods at 19.5 taels. It is heard that export groups are also buying up goods these days, so the market prospects are very promising, and there may be no goods arriving within the year. Because of this, people's hearts are firmer and the standard is more stable. According to recent daily sales of more than a thousand bundles, it is feared that there will be a shortage of goods within the year. Therefore, those with abundant funds are taking advantage of the opportunity to absorb goods to prevent unexpected events in the future. Therefore, recent transactions feel more lively.

Silk and Tea Sales of Sichuan and Hanzhong Silk Waste Slightly Increase to France 222

Since autumn, sales of Sichuan and Hanzhong silk waste to Europe have been sluggish for a long time. Stocks in Shanghai are increasing daily, and prices are weakening. Recently, winter silk fabrics have been launched overseas, and silk weaving factories are preparing to start weaving for spring. Demand is gradually rising. Shanghai French firms have been receiving inquiries from Paris, Marseille, Lyon, and other places in recent days. The Sichuan and Hanzhong silk waste market will invite Chinese merchants to negotiate today during the Autumn Races. However, it is heard that the overseas prices of Xi'an Wan Shou silk and Sichuan scarves are still trending weaker.

The Silk Market in Foreign Firms Is Declining 223

Yesterday was Wednesday, the third day of the Autumn Races. Foreign firms only worked in the morning. The number of overseas silk telegrams to Shanghai was sparse. Silk factories were all closed, and manufacturers were increasingly negative. The market atmosphere was stagnant. Yesterday, only Samsung imported 8 bales of Bai Gan silk, and Xiang Ji imported 10 bales of cotton Zhou Bai silk. Prices were all firm.

The Tea Market During the Autumn Races 224

Yesterday, the tea market in Shanghai foreign firms was still quiet. Foreign firms only have half a day of market hours during the Autumn Races, and the Russian Association for Assistance has always maintained an attitude of not buying unless prices are low and is very picky. Therefore, there were no large transactions of Zhen Mei Gong Xi green tea and Qimen black tea in the market yesterday.

Piece Goods Chinese and Foreign Goods Are Trending Weak 225

The cloth market in this factory is gradually turning soft, especially fine cloth and fine twill, which are showing a persistent downward trend. The reason is that the market has been gradually rising since the beginning of spring and has never fallen back. At the beginning of last month, the opening prices were already at their highest point, so once actual sales were quiet, people's hearts were extremely weak. Fine cloth was the first to fall, and fine twill has been falling steadily in recent days. Yesterday, Yang He fell again, selling for 6 taels and 9.25 qian. Lan Shuang Yu was 6 taels and 7.5 qian. The rising trend of coarse cloth has also stopped. Hubei Tian Zi has been arriving in Shanghai successively, and 13-pound Shuang Ying spots have also increased. However, coarse twill is still firm, which is because the number of goods shipped is not large.

Eastern and Western Piece Goods East goods have been falling steadily in recent days. Yesterday, Zhong Hua Rong has slightly turned around, and there are not many goods priced at 1.9 qian. Black Hua Rong must be priced at 1.925 qian. The falling trend of printed velvet has not stopped, and most have fallen to 1.9 qian. Zhong Shan Ni, after a period of stockout, has arrived yesterday. Jiao Ye Ti Shu is 2.8 qian, and Yin Pao Che is 3.9 qian. This street has added purchases. Gui Jiao Bi Ji and fine Bi Ji have gradually arrived in Shanghai, so the trend is not as firm as before. Xia Shen Zhi Gong Ni has also arrived in 40-50 pieces, and Jing An Si Ma Gu Xi Shou are both opening at 2.9 qian. Since the numbers at Xiao Dong Men once searched for Cai Tiao Rong, it has risen yesterday, and most are opening outside at 6.5 taels.

Six Hundred Tons of Soybeans Loaded for Southeast Asia, Three Thousand Tons Shipped to Germany and the Netherlands

Within the past eight days last week, Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, and Nisshin have shipped a total of 43,344 bags of white sugar to the Yangtze River. In addition, 12,463 pieces of kelp were shipped.

Shanghai Market

Market News 247

The Shanghai China Jockey Club, located at 770 Jing'an Temple Road, announces that the Gold Cup Grand Prix will be held on December 7th in Yinxiang Township. The Gold Cup is valued at over ten thousand gold pieces and will be awarded to the winning horse. Therefore, all the top horses in Shanghai's three major racing clubs are considered prime contenders. Horses such as Face Off, Kaituo, St. Leader, Tuoyi, Fushi, Weishoulan, Fanya Wulan, and Xu Fanlilante, etc., have all demonstrated excellent reputations in past races. The competition is expected to be fierce. The club is now issuing Gold Cup Champagne tickets, priced at five yuan each. Sales have been brisk in recent days, and it is expected that the prize money for the winning horse will rival that of the Shanghai Champagne prize.

Xinda Xiang Leather Goods Store, located inside the Xinbei Gate Main Street, announces that its reputation for fine goods and reasonable prices is well-known throughout the community. To celebrate its tenth anniversary, starting from the 6th of this month, it will be holding a major sale on all kinds of leather goods, both coarse and fine, for fifty days. The store owns its own property and does not have to pay rent, so its prices are lower than most. Free gifts will also be given away.

The Pathé Records Company, located at the intersection of Renji Road and Sichuan Road, announces that it has released the most records, with over three thousand varieties in the past decade. This month, a large batch of new records will be released. Peking opera records include: "Only Distance Tests a Horse's Strength," "Xiao He追韓信," "Taibai Gets Drunk," "Zhu Maichen," "Mother Xu Scolds Cao," "Jinshui Bridge," "Locking Five Dragons," "Lianhuan Tao," "Loyalty and Filial Piety Complete," "South Heaven Gate," "Visiting Mother," "Imperial Stele Pavilion," "Sangyuan寄子," "Chopping Three Passes with a Knife," "Yanmen Pass," "Offering Sacrifices at the Pagoda," "Tiying Saves Her Father," "Baolian Deng," "Great Ascend to the Throne," "Second Entry to the Palace," "Little Shepherd Boy," "Releasing Cotton," "Visiting Relatives and Scolding Each Other," "Swinging River Boat," "Northern Han King," "Emperor Liang Wu," "Mulen Monk," "Capturing Ma Chao," "Fishing for a Golden Turtle," "Dingjun Mountain," "Crying at the Spirit Tablet," "Battle of Puguan," "Yu Zangjian," "Taking the Commander's Seal," "Scolding the Court," "Wenzhao Pass," and dozens of others. There are also a dozen or so records of Suzhou ballads, folk songs, ventriloquism, crosstalk, harmonica, storytelling, and comedic tunes.

Tongchang Silk Thread Store, located at the corner of Huajin on Erma Road, announces that it has been established for over thirty years, specializing in domestic goods and various European and American foreign goods. To reduce inventory and sell for cash, a discount department has been set up, starting from one dime. Items include needles, scented powders, scarves, stockings, wool, etc., in a variety of colors for customers to choose from. Since the discount started, ladies have been flocking to the store. Those who want to get cheap goods may want to give it a try.

The Bailin Company, located at the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Haining Road, announces that it is the most reputable department store in Shanghai, selecting and selling the latest global products. Everything is available. To celebrate its first anniversary, the store will be offering discounts on all goods starting today, holding a major sale and giveaway for one month. In addition to specially reduced prices, all goods will be further discounted by 5%, and valuable gifts will be given to show special treatment.

The Shanghai China Industrial Society announces that batteries have a wide range of sales, and have been imported from foreign countries for many years, selling well throughout China. Although there are many domestic products recently, most of them are difficult to make durable due to poor manufacturing methods, so they have failed to resist foreign goods. The company, located in Tianfu Lane, Laobazi Road, has spent several years of effort, and the battery department engineer, Mr. Hong Shangda, has invented a new method of making batteries with fine powder quality. Not only is it above ordinary domestic products, but it is even better than the most famous imported products. The opening is scheduled for the 6th, and the company will host a banquet for domestic and foreign merchants and key figures in the press to connect.

The Yongan Sock Factory, located on Dongmen Road outside Xiaodongmen, announces that since its opening, its store has been extremely crowded for one month. At this winter season, it has specially transported a variety of wool fabrics for display and sale. Today is the last day of the opening discount. Men's and women's long silk stockings are still sold for 88 cents per pair, women's long silk stockings are 70 cents per pair, and a set of moving pictures is given away for every one yuan spent.

The Dadong Sock Factory South Branch, located on Dadongmen Main Street inside Xiaodongmen, announces that the various men's and women's silk stockings produced by the factory are known for their good quality and low price. The cosmetics and daily necessities sold are especially well-prepared. This winter, a large batch of wool fabrics has arrived on the market, and the prices are low. The weather has suddenly turned cold in recent days, and the store has been very busy.

The Wenhuzhuan Kan Society, located on Sanma Road, announces that it is organized by the literary and art circles of Shanghai and publishes one issue of Wenhuzhuan Kan every month. It is a deep study of Wenhuzhuan Kan. Since its publication, it has been well received by all sectors of society. The ninth issue has now been published, and the content is more exciting than before. There are also reward riddles, and those who guess correctly will receive a small gift to help with their interest. Those who want to read this magazine should attach a two-cent stamp and write to Mr. Wu at the Sanma Road address, and one issue will be sent immediately.

The Shunfeng Brand Silk Stocking Factory, located at the north end of Sanmaoge Bridge, Qipan Street, announces that the factory's first sales venue has newly released various woolen sweaters, woolen socks, wild duck velvet socks, scarves, gloves and other seasonal clothing items. The products are new and innovative, far surpassing imported products, and the pricing is lower. It is said that in recent days, men and women who love domestic goods have been introducing each other and are happy to purchase and use them.

Medical News 248

The Jingjing Pharmacy, located at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Wangping Street, announces that since the sale of Congenital Red and other elixirs, the efficacy has been remarkable, and therefore the business has been very prosperous. The original site is not enough for office work, so it has moved to a new house at 387 Wuma Road for business, and has been greatly expanded. In addition to selling secret and experienced elixirs, it also sells new medicines from famous global factories, pharmaceutical chemical industry raw materials and supplies, as well as high-end Chinese and Western cosmetics and fragrances. Everything is available. The retail price is calculated according to the wholesale price, and the wholesale price is even more favorable. It is expected to become a highlight in the pharmaceutical industry in the future.

Book and Newspaper Introductions

Fudan Social Science Department Bi-monthly 249

— Thing

Since Mr. Ying Chengyi took over the Department of Sociology at Fudan University, the spirit within the department has been excellent, due to the work of teachers and students and the contact between alumni. Recently, the department has published a bi-monthly publication, which is very exciting in terms of content, and the price is very low. It is published on the 5th and 20th of each month. The writing is a collaboration between teachers and students.

After the first issue was published, I have read it slightly, and I feel that they have two indelible spirits, that is, equal emphasis on both academic theory and practical application. Therefore, I will make a brief introduction in this column. I think that the readers who love social sciences will also abandon hearing about it.

There are three articles in total. The first is "What is Truth" by Mr. Ying Chengyi, head of the department. The second is "Dynamic Social View" by Mr. Wang Zaiqin, an alumnus. The third is "Research on Allied Strikes" by Mr. Chen Peisen, an alumnus. The following is a brief description of each:

The article "What is Truth" is divided into four aspects for discussion. The first is "The Starting Point of Truth." The second is "The Aspect of Truth." The third is "The Complexity of Truth." The fourth is "The Ultimate of Truth." The author first determines the two elements of things and me, because human actions are based on the interaction of these two elements, which is the starting point of the production of truth. When talking about the first paragraph of "Basic Starting Point," it says, "I am the one who determines things, so when I mention myself, the meaning of things is already included in it, but I am the aspect of its expression, and things are the aspect of its connotation. Things are also the ones who determine me, so when I mention things, the meaning of me is already included in it, but things are the aspect of its expression, and I am the aspect of its connotation..." And it uses Tang poetry as an example. The second paragraph roughly says, "When people have awareness of me, they lose awareness of things. When they have awareness of things, they lose awareness of the standard." The third paragraph says that in a complex environment, human beings are not governed by me, but by things, and not governed by things, but by me. These two principles are adjusted to each other, and a kind of relationship is produced. From this relationship, I can recognize me, and from this relationship, I can recognize things. This relationship has two methods, namely natural relationship and artificial relationship, and it also explains that the relationship between me, things, and things and me are mutually conditional. The second aspect is "The Aspect of Truth" which is divided into three paragraphs for discussion, namely "The Truth of Me," which measures all things with me as the standard, "The Truth of Things," which measures many me with things as the standard, and there are many beautiful examples in it, which are omitted. The third paragraph is the truth of the relationship between me and things." The original text says, "The relationship transcends me, there is awareness of the relationship, it does not follow things, nor does it adhere to itself, and it regards things and me as one..." And it uses the relationship between husband and wife as an example. The third aspect is "The Complexity of Truth," believing that the relationship between things, me, and things and me is the three aspects of truth, not absolute truth, but embracing these three aspects and synthesizing them into one. This comprehensive nature can also assume three nouns to represent them, namely, the first cause, the second cause, and the third cause. The author says, "The third cause is the relationship between me and things. The invisible of things is the first cause, and the visible of things is the second cause..." And it uses the European War as an example. The political situation and the psychological situation are all invisible, and they are the first cause. The conflict between Austria and Serbia is visible, and it is the second cause. Therefore, the first cause is inevitable, and the second cause is probable. The third cause is also called the final cause, because "Things are born of me, and I am the final cause. I am born of things, and things are the final cause." Admitting these three causes is a cycle of reciprocity and continuous flow. This is the whole of truth. It is also the origin of religious truth, scientific truth, and philosophical truth. The author says, "...Looking at the three kinds of truth together, what is said is actually one truth. Looking at the three kinds of truth separately, they are three kinds of truth. The inability to define it in one word is not due to the inability of human learning, but to the limitation of human skills. Truth is dynamic, but language is static, and thought is static, so it is no wonder that religious scholars and scientists insist on their own opinions," The fourth aspect is about "The Ultimate of Truth," summarizing the whole article and saying that truth transcends everything, and because it transcends everything, everything is not truth, because truth is dynamic and can never be expressed in language, thought, or symbols.

The second article is "Dynamic Social View," which is divided into seven major sections. ㈠ The introduction describes three methods of observing society, namely, observing society from the universe, observing society from the individual, observing society from the society, and their criticisms. ㈡ Using science to observe the dynamics of the universe, and using the structure of celestial bodies to prove that the universe is moving. ㈢ Using science to observe the dynamics of matter, and using the atoms and electrons of matter organization to prove that the surface of static matter is also moving. ㈣ Observing the combined society from the dynamic universe, and proving the local movement of society from the entire movement of the universe. ㈤ The law of change of social phenomena, admitting that the movement of society is carried out according to Hegel's "dialectics". ㈥ is the theory of revolution in the process of social progress. A sudden change will occur in the dynamic process of society. This sudden change is commonly called revolution. It is completely a natural trend that cannot be stopped or created.

The third article is "Research on Allied Strikes". Because this article has not yet been completed, it will be introduced after it is completed.

Announcement The second issue of the bi-monthly publication will be published soon. The content includes articles by Mr. Xiao Yuan and Mr. Zhang Hongchou, an alumnus.

Manuscript Examples for Book and Newspaper Introductions 250

㈠ The text is limited to introducing the latest publications at home and abroad. In addition to literary works, all books and newspapers on politics, economy, law, science, education, etc. are included in the introduction, but boring books and newspapers will not be introduced.

㈡ The paintings are limited to the latest works of new writers at home and abroad and related illustrations to the text.

㈢ Articles on textual research or research on ancient Chinese books will not be published.

㈣ Books and photos are limited to those related to the text.

㈤ The text should not exceed 3,000 words per article at most.

㈥ Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.
